<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Street_grid">Street grid</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Miami-Dade_County,_Florida&amp;action=edit&amp;section=36" title="Edit section: Street grid">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>A <a href="/wiki/Grid_plan" title="Grid plan">street grid</a> stretches from downtown Miami throughout the county. This grid was adopted by the City of Miami following <a href="/wiki/World_War_I" title="World War I">World War I</a> after the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/United_States_Post_Office" title="United States Post Office">United States Post Office</a> threatened to cease mail deliveries in the city because the original system of named streets, with names often changing every few blocks and multiple streets in the city sharing the same name, was too confusing for the mail carriers.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-76"><a href="#cite_note-76">[76]</a></sup> The new grid was later extended throughout the county as the population grew west, south, and north of city limits. The grid is laid out with Miami Avenue as the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Meridian_(PLSS)" title="Meridian (PLSS)">meridian</a> going North-South and Flagler Street the <a href="/wiki/Baseline_(surveying)" title="Baseline (surveying)">baseline</a> going east-west. The grid is primarily numerical so that, for example, all street addresses north of Flagler and west of Miami Avenue have <b>NW</b> in their address (e.g. NW 27th Avenue). Because its point of origin is in downtown Miami which is close to the coast, the <b>NW</b> and <b>SW</b> quadrants are much larger than the <b>SE</b> and <b>NE</b> quadrants. Many roads, especially major ones, are also named, although, with a few notable exceptions, the number is in more common usage among locals. Although this grid is easy to understand once one is oriented to it, it is not universal in the entire county. Hialeah uses its own grid system which is entirely different in its orientation. Coral Gables and Miami Lakes use named streets almost exclusively, and various smaller municipalities such as Florida City and Homestead use their own grid system along with the Miami-Dade grid system adding to the confusion. In the beach cities and parks of Miami Beach, Surfside, Bal Harbor, Haulover, Sunny Isles, and Golden Beach, the streets are coordinated with the main grid; however, their avenues are named.</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Sports_venues">Sports venues</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Miami-Dade_County,_Florida&amp;action=edit&amp;section=42" title="Edit section: Sports venues">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:202px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:MarlinPark.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1675" data-file-width="2592" height="129" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/d/df/MarlinPark.jpg/200px-MarlinPark.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/d/df/MarlinPark.jpg/300px-MarlinPark.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/d/df/MarlinPark.jpg/400px-MarlinPark.jpg 2x" width="200"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:MarlinPark.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
<a href="/wiki/Marlins_Park" title="Marlins Park">Marlins Park</a>, home of the <a href="/wiki/Miami_Marlins" title="Miami Marlins">Miami Marlins</a>.</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:202px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:AAAMiami.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="958" data-file-width="1278" height="150" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e8/AAAMiami.jpg/200px-AAAMiami.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e8/AAAMiami.jpg/300px-AAAMiami.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e8/AAAMiami.jpg/400px-AAAMiami.jpg 2x" width="200"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:AAAMiami.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
<a href="/wiki/American_Airlines_Arena" title="American Airlines Arena">American Airlines Arena</a>, home of the <a href="/wiki/Miami_Heat" title="Miami Heat">Miami Heat</a>.</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:202px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Dolphinstadiumvikes.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2134" data-file-width="2848" height="150" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bf/Dolphinstadiumvikes.jpg/200px-Dolphinstadiumvikes.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bf/Dolphinstadiumvikes.jpg/300px-Dolphinstadiumvikes.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bf/Dolphinstadiumvikes.jpg/400px-Dolphinstadiumvikes.jpg 2x" width="200"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Dolphinstadiumvikes.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sun_Life_Stadium" title="Sun Life Stadium">Sun Life Stadium</a>, home of the <a href="/wiki/Miami_Dolphins" title="Miami Dolphins">Miami Dolphins</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Miami_Hurricanes" title="Miami Hurricanes">Miami Hurricanes</a>.</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>Miami-Dade County holds the majority of sports arenas, stadiums and complexes in <a href="/wiki/South_Florida" title="South Florida">South Florida</a>. Some of these sports facilities are:</p>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sun_Life_Stadium" title="Sun Life Stadium">Sun Life Stadium</a>- <a href="/wiki/Miami_Dolphins" title="Miami Dolphins">Miami Dolphins</a> (football) and The <a href="/wiki/Miami_Hurricanes" title="Miami Hurricanes">Miami Hurricanes</a> (football),</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Marlins_Park" title="Marlins Park">Marlins Park</a> – <a href="/wiki/Miami_Marlins" title="Miami Marlins">Miami Marlins</a> (baseball)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/American_Airlines_Arena" title="American Airlines Arena">American Airlines Arena</a>- <a href="/wiki/Miami_Heat" title="Miami Heat">Miami Heat</a> (basketball)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Tennis_Center_at_Crandon_Park" title="Tennis Center at Crandon Park">Tennis Center at Crandon Park</a>- <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sony_Ericcson_Open" title="Sony Ericcson Open">Sony Ericcson Open</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/FIU_Stadium" title="FIU Stadium">FIU Stadium</a>- <a href="/wiki/FIU_Panthers_football" title="FIU Panthers football">FIU Panthers</a> (football)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/FIU_Arena" title="FIU Arena">FIU Arena</a>- <a href="/wiki/FIU_Panthers_men%27s_basketball" title="FIU Panthers men's basketball">FIU Panthers</a> (basketball)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/FIU_Baseball_Stadium" title="FIU Baseball Stadium">FIU Baseball Stadium</a>- FIU Panthers (baseball)</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/BankUnited_Center" title="BankUnited Center">BankUnited Center</a>- Miami Hurricanes (basketball)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Tropical_Park_Stadium" title="Tropical Park Stadium">Tropical Park Stadium</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Homestead-Miami_Speedway" title="Homestead-Miami Speedway">Homestead-Miami Speedway</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Calder_Race_Course" title="Calder Race Course">Calder Race Course</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Hialeah_Park_Race_Track" title="Hialeah Park Race Track">Hialeah Park Race Track</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Alex_Rodriguez_Park_at_Mark_Light_Field" title="Alex Rodriguez Park at Mark Light Field">Alex Rodriguez Park at Mark Light Field</a>- Miami Hurricanes (baseball)</li>
</ul>
<p>Former venues include:</p>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Bobby_Maduro_Miami_Stadium" title="Bobby Maduro Miami Stadium">Bobby Maduro Miami Stadium</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Miami_Arena" title="Miami Arena">Miami Arena</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Miami_Orange_Bowl" title="Miami Orange Bowl">Miami Orange Bowl</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Miami_Marine_Stadium" title="Miami Marine Stadium">Miami Marine Stadium</a></li>
</ul>
<p>Planned:</p>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Miami_MLS_Stadium" title="Miami MLS Stadium">Miami MLS Stadium</a></li>
</ul>
